## Section 001: Visual Explainer Skill Patterns
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 001 "Visual Explainer Skill Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed no seed line conveys that this theme holds a single 168-line personal 202603 skill that turns codebase explanation into a produced artifact, an interactive scrollable HTML page built from a five-part process, agent-driven code exploration, act-structured narrative, mandatory pedagogy, template-based generation, and a fixed output location with browser preview
- **supporting_reason:** Section 001 "Visual Explainer Skill Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the skill exists because documentation defaults to boring and unread, its when-to-use list literally includes documentation that is not boring, so it replaces prose docs with a designed reading experience, metaphors, progressive disclosure, and visual variety doing what walls of text do not
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 001 "Visual Explainer Skill Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: reading the theme as a styling guide misses its ordering, the process spends its first stage entirely on code understanding, the bold rule forbidding a single word of explanation before deep exploration, presentation being the last mile of a comprehension pipeline
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 001 "Visual Explainer Skill Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: this reference covers the explainer-production practice, the code-exploration machinery it launches belongs to the exploration themes
- **revision_decision:** Section 001 "Visual Explainer Skill Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to open with the single-source inventory, the artifact-not-answer framing, and the understanding-before-writing rule
